ag hn ai aj\"><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf hu hv paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy ho\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"ih ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*U2m9OXX-S7pHrj4G3qgCAg.png?q=20\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/3242/1*U2m9OXX-S7pHrj4G3qgCAg.png\" width=\"1621\" height=\"912\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*U2m9OXX-S7pHrj4G3qgCAg.png 276w, nofollow\">Icons 8</a></figcaption></figure></div></div></div><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"ab ac ae af ag dk ai aj\"><h1 id=\"9fc3\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">What is a dashboard?</h1><p id=\"4a69\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki df ek\">A dashboard is a view of carefully selected information. In cars, it is a visualization of our speed, the oil and fuel level, and other important information to steer the vehicle. Of course, in newer cars, we might have a lot more information on the dashboard.</p><p id=\"4303\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">Why do we use dashboards? There are several reasons, which we can boil down to three points:</p><ol class=\"\"><li id=\"9afd\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">We want to see the big picture.</li><li id=\"8f3f\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">We want to focus on specific metrics or pieces of information that are important to our business.</li><li id=\"3705\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">We want to be able to deep dive into the information so that we can see what action needs to be taken.</li></ol><blockquote class=\"kw kx ky\"><p id=\"8164\" class=\"jp jq kz jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">A dashboard is a visual display of the most important information needed to achieve one or more objectives, consolidated and arranged on a single screen so the information can be monitored at a glance. — Stephen Few</p></blockquote><h2 id=\"6200\" class=\"la is dn ce it lb lc eo ix ld le er jb es lf eu jf ev lg ex jj ey lh fa jn li ek\">What does a B2B dashboard show?</h2><p id=\"e305\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki df ek\">This depends on a lot of different factors. But most importantly, a dashboard shows what is important to your business or department. Because what is important to me might not be important to you.</p><h1 id=\"7bd1\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">Know your audience</h1><p id=\"c77a\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki df ek\">To communicate in the best way possible, one needs to know their audience. Turning it down a notch might seems like losing what you are trying to communicate. However, by thinking in simple terms, nothing will be lost as long as you are still true to the complexity of the problem.</p><blockquote class=\"kw kx ky\"><p id=\"f002\" class=\"jp jq kz jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">“Simplicity is not the opposite of complexity: complexity is a fact of the world, whereas simplicity is in the mind.“ —Stephen Few, <a href=\"https://www.perceptualedge.com/blog/?p=903\" class=\"ck iq\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Simplicity vs. Complexity: Designing Goals</a></p></blockquote><p id=\"2611\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">Knowing to whom you are speaking is knowing your audience. Of course, we are talking about communicating data, and therefore who will read this data you’re presenting. But when communicating data, there are many factors to take into account. Where the good consultant would say, “Problem, consequence, solution,” we can take it down a notch. I think most of this can be answered by asking:</p><ul class=\"\"><li id=\"45db\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\"><strong class=\"jr lk\">Who</strong> is the reader</li><li id=\"5d70\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\"><strong class=\"jr lk\">What</strong> are we communicating?</li><li id=\"c19f\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\"><strong class=\"jr lk\">How</strong> are we communicating this?</li></ul><h1 id=\"5173\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">Who</h1></div></div><div class=\"hf\"><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"hg hh hi hj hk hl af hm ag hn ai aj\"><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf hu hv paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy ho\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"ih ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png?q=20\" width=\"1621\" height=\"912\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"1621\" height=\"912\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/3242/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png\" width=\"1621\" height=\"912\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1456/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png 728w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1632/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png 816w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1808/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png 904w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1984/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png 992w, https://miro.medium.com/max/2000/1*Si0YKnwUpC1xzy3Q7g-1Kw.png 1000w\" sizes=\"1000px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div><figcaption class=\"im in cz cx cy io ip ce b ft cg ch\">Illustration by <a href=\"https://icons8.com/\" class=\"ck iq\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Icons 8</a></figcaption></figure></div></div></div><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"ab ac ae af ag dk ai aj\"><p id=\"8e7b\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">Who will read and decipher what you are writing or putting into a perfectly designed graph? What kind of person has stumbled upon your wonder of a graph, which you think should be up for nomination for a design award? Is it someone who is used to reading these kinds of visualizations? Or an elderly person who found your graph through their grandchild? Does the person know about your data?</p><p id=\"0ad3\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">Here it is also important to take the group’s level of maturity as well as literacy into account because it might have an impact on how people are using the tools we are given them. Who we are communicating with is an essential question. Since we want our message to get through, but cannot make a clear communication for everyone, we need to make a cut and select a group.</p><blockquote class=\"ll\"><p id=\"58ab\" class=\"lm ln dn do b lo lp lq lr ls lt ki ch\">The representation and presentation of data to facilitate understanding. — Andy Kirk</p></blockquote><p id=\"1aac\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em lu iw jt ep lv ja jv jw lw jy jz ka lx kc kd ke ly kg kh ki df ek\">Let’s say our audience is only C-Level, then we need to know something about how they work, how much time they have on their hands, and what they would like or need to see. The way we communicate with an expert in the field is very different from the way we communicate with someone with little knowledge on the subject. If we are the ones with the data, and we want people to see, decipher, and read our work, we need to communicate strategically and effectively.</p><h1 id=\"9988\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">What and how</h1><p id=\"2bff\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki df ek\">In a B2B context, how we communicate core business data using this dashboard can be structured. To illustrate this we can use Stephen Few’s different dashboard types as found in his book: <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/dp/1938377001/ref=pd_lpo_sbs_dp_ss_1?pf_rd_p=aeebc627-7ecf-4129-8c0c-1d437f271eca&amp;pf_rd_s=lpo-top-stripe-1&amp;pf_rd_t=201&amp;pf_rd_i=0596100167&amp;pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_r=DA9FH77F269WWARN4ERP&amp;pf_rd_r=DA9FH77F269WWARN4ERP&amp;pf_rd_p=aeebc627-7ecf-4129-8c0c-1d437f271eca\" class=\"ck iq\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\"><em class=\"kz\">Information Dashboard Design.</em></a></p><ul class=\"\"><li id=\"c6be\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\"><strong class=\"jr lk\">Strategic</strong></li><li id=\"f5c2\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\"><strong class=\"jr lk\">Operational</strong></li><li id=\"d16d\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\"><strong class=\"jr lk\">Analytical</strong></li></ul><p id=\"98f6\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">Stephen Few’s division of the dashboards is not made to suit a specific kind of business but is rather a way of structuring the communication. Knowing what type of data and information you want to communicate leaves you with what kind of dashboard you should use. That said, when you know the rules you can break them, and truth be told I do some mixing of the strategic and the operational in my line of work.</p><p id=\"4566\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">The dashboard types are divided into three different categories, where details and level of information grow as we progress downwards. The same actually can be used when designing for different target groups.</p><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf cx cy paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy lz\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"ma ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*kI0-hKdVbq2M3BhaUZp30g.png?q=20\" width=\"992\" height=\"622\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"992\" height=\"622\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/1984/1*kI0-hKdVbq2M3BhaUZp30g.png\" width=\"992\" height=\"622\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*kI0-hKdVbq2M3BhaUZp30g.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*kI0-hKdVbq2M3BhaUZp30g.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*kI0-hKdVbq2M3BhaUZp30g.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1400/1*kI0-hKdVbq2M3BhaUZp30g.png 700w\" sizes=\"700px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div><figcaption class=\"im in cz cx cy io ip ce b ft cg ch\">How to structure information and what type of dashboard to use when communicating with your target group.</figcaption></figure><p id=\"4631\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">The figure above shows three different pyramids: <em class=\"kz\">The company hierarchy</em> or how most companies are built—upper management on top and roles become more specialized as we progress down the ranks. <em class=\"kz\">The information hierarchy </em>shows a way of structuring the informational approach to each level. <em class=\"kz\">The dashboard design</em> shows how we can design for them.</p><p id=\"8467\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">The further up we go, the shorter the selection of data, visualization, and information, however, not less important. The further down we go, the more details, and fewer conclusions; in other words, you have the exploratory analysis in the bottom of the triangle, and the explanatory on the top. We can use this when we communicate with different stakeholders. If we applied the same approach to the hierarchical structure of a business, we’d have: Information at the top are big numbers and clear communication of how the business or department overall performs, and the level of detail in the business intelligence grows as we progress downwards.</p><h1 id=\"d581\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">The Three Types of Dashboards</h1><h1 id=\"5cbf\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">The Strategic Dashboard</h1></div></div><div class=\"hf\"><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"hg hh hi hj hk hl af hm ag hn ai aj\"><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf hu hv paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy ah\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mb ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png?q=20\" width=\"1096\" height=\"826\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"1096\" height=\"826\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/2192/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png\" width=\"1096\" height=\"826\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1456/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png 728w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1632/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png 816w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1808/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png 904w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1984/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png 992w, https://miro.medium.com/max/2000/1*QVUevCh6sMBXs-rLDUqdlA.png 1000w\" sizes=\"1000px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div><figcaption class=\"im in cz cx cy io ip ce b ft cg ch\">An example of a strategic dashboard. <a href=\"http://datastudio.google.com/reporting/d17b2d68-2947-4a35-8b82-7d3c500725c4\" class=\"ck iq\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Click to see a live view of the report</a></figcaption></figure></div></div></div><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"ab ac ae af ag dk ai aj\"><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf md me gr mf mg mh mi mj az mk ml mm mn mo mp paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mc\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mq ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*DD-DyRGA3_SOBFbeKvLRrA.gif?q=20\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/1200/1*DD-DyRGA3_SOBFbeKvLRrA.gif\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*DD-DyRGA3_SOBFbeKvLRrA.gif 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1000/1*DD-DyRGA3_SOBFbeKvLRrA.gif 500w\" sizes=\"500px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><p id=\"e344\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">The strategic dashboard provides us with primary key performance indicators (KPIs). This dashboard should only give “The Big Numbers,” and should also be easy to read and comprehend, and fast to decipher.</p><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf md me gr mf mg mh mi mj az mk ml mm mn mo mp paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mc\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mq ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*hDcjWp-I7QCAc8aj_jaaQA.gif?q=20\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/1200/1*hDcjWp-I7QCAc8aj_jaaQA.gif\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*hDcjWp-I7QCAc8aj_jaaQA.gif 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1000/1*hDcjWp-I7QCAc8aj_jaaQA.gif 500w\" sizes=\"500px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div><figcaption class=\"im in cz cx cy io ip ce b ft cg ch\">Always show numbers against a target creates a context to the value</figcaption></figure><p id=\"5d1e\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">This type of dashboard does not go into detail and has the sole purpose of communicating important information fast.</p><p id=\"9746\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">It aims to show the current state of the entire company and could easily include data on how the company performs across several divisions or departments. One could say that this would show the CMO where to look for further information.</p><h2 id=\"f518\" class=\"la is dn ce it lb lc eo ix ld le er jb es lf eu jf ev lg ex jj ey lh fa jn li ek\">What visualizations to use in the strategic dashboard?</h2><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf md me gr mf mg mh mi mj az mk ml mm mn mo mp paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mc\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mq ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*usDj1CITnNcU6Himkadptw.gif?q=20\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/1200/1*usDj1CITnNcU6Himkadptw.gif\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*usDj1CITnNcU6Himkadptw.gif 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1000/1*usDj1CITnNcU6Himkadptw.gif 500w\" sizes=\"500px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><p id=\"d801\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">Another way of showing the overview is to show trends using line graphs or sparklines. The key using simple graphs is to not use too many details.</p><h2 id=\"79f6\" class=\"la is dn ce it lb lc eo ix ld le er jb es lf eu jf ev lg ex jj ey lh fa jn li ek\"><strong class=\"ay\">Key Features of the Strategic Dashboard</strong></h2><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf md me gr mf mg mh mi mj az mk ml mm mn mo mp paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mc\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mq ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*k0CiuL_tGTYY1RbGNiocQA.gif?q=20\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/1200/1*k0CiuL_tGTYY1RbGNiocQA.gif\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*k0CiuL_tGTYY1RbGNiocQA.gif 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1000/1*k0CiuL_tGTYY1RbGNiocQA.gif 500w\" sizes=\"500px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><ul class=\"\"><li id=\"4e5c\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">We want to see performance over time.</li><li id=\"3292\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">It shows KPI performance with references to benchmarks. The data is often compared to performance at a different time (e.g. last year).</li><li id=\"9c6a\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">Often multiple sources are used to create the <em class=\"kz\">complete picture.</em></li></ul><h1 id=\"9524\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">The Operational Dashboard</h1></div></div><div class=\"hf\"><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"hg hh hi hj hk hl af hm ag hn ai aj\"><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf hu hv paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mr\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"ms ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png?q=20\" width=\"1206\" height=\"912\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"1206\" height=\"912\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/2412/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png\" width=\"1206\" height=\"912\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1456/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png 728w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1632/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png 816w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1808/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png 904w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1984/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png 992w, https://miro.medium.com/max/2000/1*9HwXY5sO_ebDCvyBr-w5Xg.png 1000w\" sizes=\"1000px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div><figcaption class=\"im in cz cx cy io ip ce b ft cg ch\">An example of an operational dashboard. <a href=\"http://datastudio.google.com/reporting/9f036a79-461a-4956-897d-71b779569a06\" class=\"ck iq\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Click to see a live version of the report</a></figcaption></figure></div></div></div><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"ab ac ae af ag dk ai aj\"><p id=\"9436\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\"><em class=\"kz\">The operational dashboard</em> oversees, you guessed it, operations. In the above example, this oversees web traffic. It aims to show the current state of a department, product, or even a specific metric that the business is using as a KPI. This could be Sessions if you are looking at web analytics. These dashboards usually offer a little more detail in the data, and digging deeper into the data, or drill-down, can also be found. To see an operational dashboard, just picture how a large factory machine would oversee their production.</p><p id=\"d31f\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">The operational dashboard above shows some of the same metrics as shown in the strategic dashboard with a deeper dive into the data. Where the C-Level would like to see <strong class=\"jr lk\">how </strong>it goes with the big numbers, the managers might want to see <strong class=\"jr lk\">what </strong>goes with the numbers.</p><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf md me gr mf mg mh mi mj az mk ml mm mn mo mp paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mc\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mq ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*UnMlOYj1-NJFCIvkoPCo1w.gif?q=20\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/1200/1*UnMlOYj1-NJFCIvkoPCo1w.gif\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*UnMlOYj1-NJFCIvkoPCo1w.gif 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1000/1*UnMlOYj1-NJFCIvkoPCo1w.gif 500w\" sizes=\"500px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><h2 id=\"bfb2\" class=\"la is dn ce it lb lc eo ix ld le er jb es lf eu jf ev lg ex jj ey lh fa jn li ek\"><strong class=\"ay\">Key Features of the Operational Dashboard</strong></h2><ul class=\"\"><li id=\"1ecc\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">Show the supporting information for the company.</li><li id=\"dba3\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">Make use of more detailed graphs. Users have first-hand knowledge of the data.</li><li id=\"f470\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">Show a cause of why the big numbers look the way they do.</li></ul><h1 id=\"358f\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">The Analytical Dashboard</h1></div></div><div class=\"hf\"><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"hg hh hi hj hk hl af hm ag hn ai aj\"><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf hu hv paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mt\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mu ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"dashboard as an example of how an analytical dashboard could be designed\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png?q=20\" width=\"1209\" height=\"909\"/></div><img alt=\"dashboard as an example of how an analytical dashboard could be designed\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"1209\" height=\"909\"/><noscript><img alt=\"dashboard as an example of how an analytical dashboard could be designed\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/2418/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png\" width=\"1209\" height=\"909\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1456/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png 728w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1632/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png 816w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1808/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png 904w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1984/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png 992w, https://miro.medium.com/max/2000/1*Nyu1lKf1pcFtNXHCWhzxEw.png 1000w\" sizes=\"1000px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div><figcaption class=\"im in cz cx cy io ip ce b ft cg ch\">An example of an analytical dashboard. There is a lot of information, however, not many conclusions. I made this to create an exploratory dashboard, where the answers can be found by deep diving. <a href=\"http://datastudio.google.com/reporting/ad123c85-730b-4413-abb2-8117e9b4bd1b\" class=\"ck iq\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Click here for a live version of the report</a></figcaption></figure></div></div></div><div class=\"n p\"><div class=\"ab ac ae af ag dk ai aj\"><p id=\"01fe\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">The analytical dashboard aims to allow the user to make their explorative data analysis. This often means very granulated data, and it is where the specialist is working. This dashboard could be complete access to a DWH (Data Warehouse), where comparing different metrics and dimensions can uncover important information for the business.</p><blockquote class=\"ll\"><p id=\"6824\" class=\"lm ln dn do b lo lp lq lr ls lt ki ch\">If you are using your data to identify certain trends that could have an impact on future decisions, you might be making an analytic dashboard.</p></blockquote><p id=\"d0ce\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em lu iw jt ep lv ja jv jw lw jy jz ka lx kc kd ke ly kg kh ki df ek\">An interesting feature of analytical dashboards is that it is not designed to explain data per se, but rather to nudge the users to use the existing data to find new insights; where the other two types of dashboards are more explanatory, the analytical dashboard is exploratory.</p><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf md me gr mf mg mh mi mj az mk ml mm mn mo mp paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mc\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mq ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*9Q3CG3JgdXeQ-YEJ0IzKbA.gif?q=20\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/1200/1*9Q3CG3JgdXeQ-YEJ0IzKbA.gif\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*9Q3CG3JgdXeQ-YEJ0IzKbA.gif 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1000/1*9Q3CG3JgdXeQ-YEJ0IzKbA.gif 500w\" sizes=\"500px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><h2 id=\"88e1\" class=\"la is dn ce it lb lc eo ix ld le er jb es lf eu jf ev lg ex jj ey lh fa jn li ek\"><strong class=\"ay\">Key Features of the Analytical Dashboard</strong></h2><ul class=\"\"><li id=\"c12f\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">Make it possible to compare and contrast multiple variables</li><li id=\"6737\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">Help users filter data, compare performance over time, and find a correlation between actions.</li><li id=\"38c2\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">Slicing and dicing the data in a structured way allow the user to determine what efforts have worked.</li><li id=\"4a36\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki lj kp kq ek\">An open dashboard where the users are given a <em class=\"kz\">data playground</em>.</li></ul><h1 id=\"8974\" class=\"ir is dn ce it iu iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo ek\">Final Thoughts</h1><h2 id=\"9078\" class=\"la is dn ce it lb lc eo ix ld le er jb es lf eu jf ev lg ex jj ey lh fa jn li ek\">Keep information concise</h2><p id=\"3212\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki df ek\">We should aim to use graphs that show a clear relationship between <strong class=\"jr lk\"><em class=\"kz\">what has been done</em></strong><em class=\"kz\"> </em>and what <strong class=\"jr lk\"><em class=\"kz\">we aim for</em></strong>. This is often referred to as <em class=\"kz\">data enrichment. </em>Of course, this is not an obligatory drill, however, in my opinion, most dashboards fall short on one thing: They only show <strong class=\"jr lk\">vanity</strong> KPIs.</p><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf md me gr mf mg mh mi mj az mk ml mm mn mo mp paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"cx cy mv\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"mw ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Vanity metrics vs Actionable Metrics\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*3w3ho1-jvf4cR_dhTsEOwQ.png?q=20\" width=\"608\" height=\"416\"/></div><img alt=\"Vanity metrics vs Actionable Metrics\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"608\" height=\"416\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Vanity metrics vs Actionable Metrics\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/1216/1*3w3ho1-jvf4cR_dhTsEOwQ.png\" width=\"608\" height=\"416\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*3w3ho1-jvf4cR_dhTsEOwQ.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1000/1*3w3ho1-jvf4cR_dhTsEOwQ.png 500w\" sizes=\"500px\"/></noscript></div></div></div></div><figcaption class=\"im in cz cx cy io ip ce b ft cg ch\">Vanity metrics vs Actionable metrics</figcaption></figure><blockquote class=\"ll\"><p id=\"f2a5\" class=\"lm ln dn do b lo mx my mz na nb ki ch\">Vanity metrics are metrics that make you look good to others but do not help you understand your own performance in a way that informs future strategies.</p></blockquote><p id=\"809e\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em lu iw jt ep lv ja jv jw lw jy jz ka lx kc kd ke ly kg kh ki df ek\">We are designing data cockpits that show a complete overview of our company activities. Hence, we do not want unnecessary information, but rather insights we can quickly turn into actions. An easy way to spot a vanity metric, is to ask <em class=\"kz\">“Can this metric lead to a course of action or inform a decision?” </em>If you can answer is “No” or you cannot tell, then there is a good chance you are dealing with a vanity metric and you probably need to re-evaluate it<em class=\"kz\">.</em></p><h2 id=\"6df5\" class=\"la is dn ce it lb lc eo ix ld le er jb es lf eu jf ev lg ex jj ey lh fa jn li ek\">Designing Dashboards</h2><p id=\"d294\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki df ek\">All in all, there is a lot of good information about designing dashboards, however, in the end, it comes down to two things: How we represent the data and make it into information, and how we structure these representations to create natural ease for the reader.</p><p id=\"6f01\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki df ek\">However, there is no “one size fits all.” Depending on your business, you might take inspiration in others’ work because they are reporting on the same KPIs as you. It is important to remember that we communicate with different people, and what one person might find amazing, might seem too academic for others. When designing dashboards remember:</p><ol class=\"\"><li id=\"a232\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kj iw jt ep kk ja jv jw kl jy jz ka km kc kd ke kn kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">See the big picture</li><li id=\"bf5b\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Focus on the specific items of information that need attention.</li><li id=\"5a2e\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Quickly drill into additional information that is needed to take action.</li></ol><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf cx cy paragraph-image\"><div class=\"cx cy nc\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"nd ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/46/0*q0AmzbeWfF0-I8pN?q=20\" width=\"300\" height=\"388\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"300\" height=\"388\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/600/0*q0AmzbeWfF0-I8pN\" width=\"300\" height=\"388\" srcSet=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/552/0*q0AmzbeWfF0-I8pN 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/600/0*q0AmzbeWfF0-I8pN 300w\" sizes=\"300px\"/></noscript></div></div></div><figcaption class=\"im in cz cx cy io ip ce b ft cg ch\">Stephen Few: Information Dashboard Design (Book cover)</figcaption></figure><h2 id=\"2d57\" class=\"la is dn ce it lb lc eo ix ld le er jb es lf eu jf ev lg ex jj ey lh fa jn li ek\">Bonus Information: Stephen Few’s 13 Pitfalls in Designing Dashboards</h2><ol class=\"\"><li id=\"e04c\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em js iw jt ep ju ja jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Exceeding the boundaries of a single screen</li><li id=\"433f\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Supplying inadequate context for the data</li><li id=\"6a8b\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Displaying excessive detail or precision</li><li id=\"d15b\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Expressing measures indirectly</li><li id=\"47bd\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Choosing inappropriate media of display</li><li id=\"9669\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Introducing meaningless variety</li><li id=\"4912\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Using poorly designed display media</li><li id=\"ccc2\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Encoding quantitative data inaccurately</li><li id=\"3b56\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Arranging the data poorly</li><li id=\"dba1\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Ineffectively highlighting what’s important</li><li id=\"0413\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Cluttering the screen with useless decoration</li><li id=\"5af7\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Misusing or overusing color</li><li id=\"f6c1\" class=\"jp jq dn jr b em kr iw jt ep ks ja jv jw kt jy jz ka ku kc kd ke kv kg kh ki ko kp kq ek\">Designing an unappealing visual display</li></ol></div></div><div class=\"hf aj\"><figure class=\"hp hq hr hs ht hf aj paragraph-image\"><div role=\"button\" tabindex=\"0\" class=\"hw hx fh hy aj hz\"><div class=\"if s fh ig\"><div class=\"ne ii s\"><div class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj bk id ie\"><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj ij ik il\" src=\"https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*PVUYcm-KSNol0-BwhqGm5Q.jpeg?q=20\" width=\"4000\" height=\"536\"/></div><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"ia ib t u v ic aj c\" width=\"4000\" height=\"536\"/><noscript><img alt=\"Image for post\" class=\"t u v ic aj\"       "text/plain": [
       "'Who will read and decipher what you are writing or putting into a perfectly designed graph? What kind of person has stumbled upon your wonder of a graph, which you think should be up for nomination for a design award? Is it someone who is used to reading these kinds of visualizations? Or an elderly person who found your graph through their grandchild? Does the person know about your data?\\n\\nHere it is also important to take the group’s level of maturity as well as literacy into account because it might have an impact on how people are using the tools we are given them. Who we are communicating with is an essential question. Since we want our message to get through, but cannot make a clear communication for everyone, we need to make a cut and select a group.\\n\\nThe representation and presentation of data to facilitate understanding. — Andy Kirk\\n\\nLet’s say our audience is only C-Level, then we need to know something about how they work, how much time they have on their hands, and what they would like or need to see. The way we communicate with an expert in the field is very different from the way we communicate with someone with little knowledge on the subject. If we are the ones with the data, and we want people to see, decipher, and read our work, we need to communicate strategically and effectively.\\n\\nWhat and how\\n\\nIn a B2B context, how we communicate core business data using this dashboard can be structured. To illustrate this we can use Stephen Few’s different dashboard types as found in his book: Information Dashboard Design.\\n\\nStrategic\\n\\nOperational\\n\\nAnalytical\\n\\nStephen Few’s division of the dashboards is not made to suit a specific kind of business but is rather a way of structuring the communication. Knowing what type of data and information you want to communicate leaves you with what kind of dashboard you should use. That said, when you know the rules you can break them, and truth be told I do some mixing of the strategic and the operational in my line of work.\\n\\nThe dashboard types are divided into three different categories, where details and level of information grow as we progress downwards. The same actually can be used when designing for different target groups.\\n\\nHow to structure information and what type of dashboard to use when communicating with your target group.\\n\\nThe figure above shows three different pyramids: The company hierarchy or how most companies are built—upper management on top and roles become more specialized as we progress down the ranks. The information hierarchy shows a way of structuring the informational approach to each level. The dashboard design shows how we can design for them.\\n\\nThe further up we go, the shorter the selection of data, visualization, and information, however, not less important. The further down we go, the more details, and fewer conclusions; in other words, you have the exploratory analysis in the bottom of the triangle, and the explanatory on the top. We can use this when we communicate with different stakeholders. If we applied the same approach to the hierarchical structure of a business, we’d have: Information at the top are big numbers and clear communication of how the business or department overall performs, and the level of detail in the business intelligence grows as we progress downwards.\\n\\nThe Three Types of Dashboards\\n\\nThe Strategic Dashboard'"
      ]

Delivery</a></li>\\n\\t</ul>\\n</li>\\n</ul>\\n</li>\\n<li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-custom menu-item-object-custom menu-item-has-children menu-item-122137\"><a href=\"#\">AWARDS</a>\\n<ul 2020</a></li>\\n</ul>\\n</li>\\n<li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-post_type menu-item-object-page menu-item-122322\"><a href=\"http://www.facebook.com/JCKmagazine\" target=\"_blank\"><i class=\"fa fa-facebook\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<li><a href=\"http://instagram.com/jckmagazine\" target=\"_blank\"><i class=\"fa fa-instagram\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<li><a href=\"https://twitter.com/JCKMagazine\" target=\"_blank\"><i class=\"fa fa-twitter\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<li><a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/user/WatchJCKTV\" target=\"_blank\"><i class=\"fa fa-youtube-play\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<li><a href=\"http://pinterest.com/jckmagazine/\" target=\"_blank\"><i class=\"fa fa-pinterest\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t</ul>\\n\\t\\t\\t</div>\\n\\t\\t</div>\\n\\t\\t<!-- END MENU -->\\n\\t\\t\\n        <!-- End Global Header -->\\n        <div role=\"main\" class=\"cf\">\\n<div id=\"infinite-article\" data-infinite=\"off\">\\n\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"post-detail-row\">\\n\\t<div class=\"row\" data-equal=\">.columns\">\\n\\t\\t<div class=\"small-12 medium-12 large-8  columns\">\\n\\t\\t\\t<article itemscope itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Article\" class=\"post post-detail post-121501 editorial-article type-editorial-article status-publish has-post-thumbnail hentry category-retail\" id=\"post-121501\" data-id=\"121501\" data-url=\"https://www.jckonline.com/editorial-article/product-descriptions-important/\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<header class=\"post-title entry-header\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"categories-container\">\\n\\t<div class=\"row\">\\n\\t\\t<aside class=\"categories small-12 medium-12 large-12 columns\"><a href=\"https://www.jckonline.com/category/news-trends/retail/\" title=\"View all posts in Retail\" >Retail</a></aside>\\n\\t</div>\\n</div>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<h1 class=\"entry-title\" itemprop=\"headline\">Product Descriptions Are as Important as Product Photos</h1>\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t</header>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<aside class=\"post-author\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<time class=\"time\" datetime=\"2021-01-27T13:02:03-05:00\" itemprop=\"datePublished\" content=\"2021-01-27T13:02:03-05:00\"> January 27, 2021</time> <em>by</em> <span itemprop=\"author\"><a href=\\'https://www.jckonline.com/writer/emili-vesilind/\\' target=\\'_blank\\'>Emili Vesilind</a></span>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t</aside>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<aside class=\"share-article hide-on-print fixed-me show-for-medium\">\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<a href=\"http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.jckonline.com%2Feditorial-article%2Fproduct-descriptions-important%2F\" class=\"boxed-icon facebook social\"><i class=\"fa fa-facebook\"></i>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t</a>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<a href=\"https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=Product+Descriptions+Are+as+Important+as+Product+Photos&url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.jckonline.com%2Feditorial-article%2Fproduct-descriptions-important%2F&via=JCKMagazine\" class=\"boxed-icon twitter social \"><i class=\"fa fa-twitter\"></i>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t</a>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/cws/share?url=https://www.jckonline.com/editorial-article/product-descriptions-important/\" class=\"boxed-icon linkedin social\"><i class=\"fa fa-linkedin\"></i>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t</a>\\n\\t\\t                <a href=\"http://pinterest.com/pin/create/link/?url=https://www.jckonline.com/editorial-article/product-descriptions-important/&media=https://www.jckonline.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Online-shopping.jpg&description=Product+Descriptions+Are+as+Important+as+Product+Photos\" class=\"boxed-icon pinterest social\" data-pin-no-hover=\"true\"><i class=\"fa fa-pinterest\"></i>\\n                                </a>\\n\\t</aside>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"post-content-container\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"post-content entry-content cf\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<span class=\\'post-content-feat-img\\'><img src=\\'https://www.jckonline.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Online-shopping.jpg\\'></span>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<p>Ask any e-commerce developer what the most important element of a product page is and they will likely say &#8220;photos.&#8221;</p>\\n<p>And they would be right. High-quality product photos are requisite to selling online. How else, if not through pictures, could a consumer understand exactly what they&#8217;re purchasing? Photos have the power to pique interest in a product at a glance, and they allow us to envision owning or wearing an item ourselves.</p>\\n<p>The bar for photos is particularly high for jewelers. Jewelry and gems are usually small, so photos must be supercrisp and lit to show tiny details. Variety is also important: A piece should be shown in silhouette and also on a human, to indicate size. All angles of a piece should be showcased in a slideshow, and photo files need to be large enough to allow consumers to zoom in for close-ups.</p>\\n<p>I&#8217;m not telling you anything you don&#8217;t know here—it&#8217;s 2021 and everyone on Earth understands that e-commerce is <a href=\"https://www.jckonline.com/editorial-article/online-returns-doubled-in-2020/\" target=\"_blank\">growing</a> like a mushroom under a wet log, and is here to stay. Thus, it goes without saying that putting your best aesthetic foot forward when selling online is important.</p>\\n<p>But while photos in jewelry e-tailing are looking sublime, product descriptions are, generally speaking, suffering. And shrinking. On too many jewelry e-comms, descriptions have been reduced to mere bullet points that relay metal type and the size of gems. When I see this on a site, I invariably think, &#8220;What a missed opportunity<em>.&#8221;</em></p>\\n<p>And sometimes there&#8217;s no description at all! This morning, for example, a cute DTC fashion jewelry collection debuted, and I eagerly clicked on the brand&#8217;s website and began perusing. The gold-tone jewelry was pretty and trendy, and a small box on the site&#8217;s homepage mentioned that the brand used vermeil. But clicking further into the site, I realized its pages were devoid of descriptions—not even dinky bulleted lists.</p>\\n<p>Because of this, visitors to the site are left to wonder if the <em>silver</em> in the product titles means &#8220;sterling silver&#8221; or just &#8220;silver tone,&#8221; and if the opal-looking gem in the middle of a beautiful ring is an actual opal or a facsimile.</p>\\n<p>The well-designed site, which is clearly targeting Gen Zers, may be an extreme example of the Great Description Decline of 2021. But it speaks to a larger trend in e-commerce that&#8217;s seen brands downsize and demote descriptions in the name of…what? Making shopping speedier? Keeping pages &#8220;cleaner&#8221;? Does it makes sense to skeletonize (or altogether delete) product description for these, or any other, reasons?</p>\\n<p>Nope. And here&#8217;s why. People don&#8217;t buy products. Not really—they buy the promise of self-improvement. And when it comes to jewelry, they buy to align themselves with certain tribes, or gain entrée into nuanced clubs (i.e., the club of women wearing trendy paper clip chains, which right now includes every Instagram influencer under the sun).</p>\\n<p>And while gorgeous photography can usher jewelry lovers into that important &#8220;want it, need it, gotta have it&#8221; mindset, a creative (but brief and fact-filled) description has the power to romance them through traditional storytelling that layers meaning and context over a piece&#8217;s basic details.</p>\\n<p>There&#8217;s a reason social media jewelry influencers such as <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/gemgossip/?hl=en\" target=\"_blank\">Gem Gossip</a>’s Danielle Miele and <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/diamondsinthelibrary/?hl=en\" target=\"_blank\">Diamonds in the Library</a>’s Becky Stone sell so much jewelry, both their own and others&#8217;: They&#8217;re masters of spinning yarns around jewelry pieces to make them seem unique, special, and exciting.</p>\\n<p>A recent Diamonds in the Library <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/p/CJ6J0nohrPn/\" target=\"_blank\">post</a> showed an antique ring from Wilson&#8217;s Estate Jewelry featuring a carving of a woman&#8217;s face. Stone&#8217;s storytelling prowess was in full effect as she wrote: &#8220;This is The Empress. <span class=\"\">Resplendent with the ethereal glory of the Art Nouveau aesthetic, she is captivating, from her opal and ruby crown to the flowing gold locks of her hair and her carefully carved hardstone face.&#8221;</span></p>\\n<p>If you&#8217;re worried about having long chunks of text gunk up your pages, consider a collapsible section; consumers receptive to being romanced by terrific writing can access the text with a single click, while those in a hurry can skip it.</p>\\n<p>But I contend that few will. Jewelry is an investment, and while impulse buys happen in brick-and-mortar stores, my feeling is that women take their time when shopping online, and enjoy revisiting photos, texts, and details on a product page multiple times before finally hitting &#8220;add to cart.&#8221;</p>\\n<p>Give ’em something tantalizing to chew on.</p>\\n<p><em>(Photo: <a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/78656956@N06/9899159484\" target=\"_blank\">HM Revenue &amp; Customs</a>)</em></p>\\n<p><em><span class=\"s2\">Follow</span> <span class=\"s2\">Emili </span><span class=\"s2\">Vesilind</span> <span class=\"s2\">on Instagram:\\xa0</span><a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/emilivesilind/\" target=\"_blank\"><span class=\"s3\">@</span><span class=\"s3\">emilivesilind</span></a></em></p>\\n<strong>Follow JCK on Instagram:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/jckmagazine/\">@jckmagazine</a><br/>\\r\\n\\r\\n<strong>Follow JCK on Twitter:</strong> <a href=\"https://twitter.com/jckmagazine\">@jckmagazine</a><br/>\\r\\n\\r\\n<strong>Follow JCK on Facebook:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/JCKmagazine\">@jckmagazine</a>\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t \\n<div class=\"category_container href=\"http://www.facebook.com/JCKmagazine\" target=\"_blank\"><i class=\"fa fa-facebook\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<li><a href=\"http://instagram.com/jckmagazine\" target=\"_blank\"><i class=\"fa fa-instagram\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<li><a href=\"https://twitter.com/JCKMagazine\" target=\"_blank\"><i class=\"fa fa-twitter\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<li><a class=\"fa fa-pinterest\"></i></a></li>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t</ul>\\n\\t\\t\\t</div>\\n\\t\\t</div>\\n\\t\\t<!-- END MENU -->\\n\\t\\t\\n        <!-- End Global Header -->\\n        <div role=\"main\" class=\"cf\">\\n<div id=\"infinite-article\" data-infinite=\"off\">\\n\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"post-detail-row\">\\n\\t<div class=\"row\" data-equal=\">.columns\">\\n\\t\\t<div class=\"small-12 medium-12 large-8  columns\">\\n\\t\\t\\t<article itemscope itemtype=\"http://schema.org/Article\" class=\"post post-detail post-121501 editorial-article type-editorial-article status-publish has-post-thumbnail hentry category-retail\" id=\"post-121501\" data-id=\"121501\" data-url=\"https://www.jckonline.com/editorial-article/product-descriptions-important/\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<header class=\"post-title entry-header\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"categories-container\">\\n\\t<div class=\"row\">\\n\\t\\t<aside class=\"categories small-12 medium-12 large-12 columns\"><a href=\"https://www.jckonline.com/category/news-trends/retail/\" title=\"View all posts in Retail\" >Retail</a></aside>\\n\\t</div>\\n</div>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<h1 class=\"entry-title\" itemprop=\"headline\">Product Descriptions Are as Important as Product Photos</h1>\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t</header>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<aside class=\"post-author\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<time class=\"time\" datetime=\"2021-01-27T13:02:03-05:00\" itemprop=\"datePublished\" content=\"2021-01-27T13:02:03-05:00\"> January 27, 2021</time> <em>by</em> <span itemprop=\"author\"><a href=\\'https://www.jckonline.com/writer/emili-vesilind/\\' target=\\'_blank\\'>Emili Vesilind</a></span>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t</aside>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<aside class=\"share-article hide-on-print fixed-me show-for-medium\">\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<a href=\"http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.jckonline.com%2Feditorial-article%2Fproduct-descriptions-important%2F\" class=\"boxed-icon facebook social\"><i class=\"fa fa-facebook\"></i>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t</a>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<a href=\"https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=Product+Descriptions+Are+as+Important+as+Product+Photos&url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.jckonline.com%2Feditorial-article%2Fproduct-descriptions-important%2F&via=JCKMagazine\" class=\"boxed-icon twitter social \"><i class=\"fa fa-twitter\"></i>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t</a>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/cws/share?url=https://www.jckonline.com/editorial-article/product-descriptions-important/\" class=\"boxed-icon linkedin social\"><i class=\"fa fa-linkedin\"></i>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t</a>\\n\\t\\t                <a href=\"http://pinterest.com/pin/create/link/?url=https://www.jckonline.com/editorial-article/product-descriptions-important/&media=https://www.jckonline.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Online-shopping.jpg&description=Product+Descriptions+Are+as+Important+as+Product+Photos\" class=\"boxed-icon pinterest social\" data-pin-no-hover=\"true\"><i class=\"fa fa-pinterest\"></i>\\n                                </a>\\n\\t</aside>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"post-content-container\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"post-content entry-content cf\" itemprop=\"articleBody\">\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<span class=\\'post-content-feat-img\\'><img src=\\'https://www.jckonline.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/Online-shopping.jpg\\'></span>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<p>Ask any e-commerce developer what the most important element of a product page is and they will likely say &#8220;photos.&#8221;</p>\\n<p>And they would be right. High-quality product photos are requisite to selling online. How else, if not through pictures, could a consumer understand exactly what they&#8217;re purchasing? Photos have the power to pique interest in a product at a glance, and they allow us to envision owning or wearing an item ourselves.</p>\\n<p>The bar for photos is particularly high for jewelers. Jewelry and gems are usually small, so photos must be supercrisp and lit to show tiny details. Variety is also important: A piece should be shown in silhouette and also on a human, to indicate size. All angles of a piece should be showcased in a slideshow, and photo files need to be large enough to allow consumers to zoom in for close-ups.</p>\\n<p>I&#8217;m not telling you anything you don&#8217;t know here—it&#8217;s 2021 and everyone on Earth understands that e-commerce is <a href=\"https://www.jckonline.com/editorial-article/online-returns-doubled-in-2020/\" target=\"_blank\">growing</a> like a mushroom under a wet log, and is here to stay. Thus, it goes without saying that putting your best aesthetic foot forward when selling online is important.</p>\\n<p>But while photos in jewelry e-tailing are looking sublime, product descriptions are, generally speaking, suffering. And shrinking. On too many jewelry e-comms, descriptions have been reduced to mere bullet points that relay metal type and the size of gems. When I see this on a site, I invariably think, &#8220;What a missed opportunity<em>.&#8221;</em></p>\\n<p>And sometimes there&#8217;s no description at all! This morning, for example, a cute DTC fashion jewelry collection debuted, and I eagerly clicked on the brand&#8217;s website and began perusing. The gold-tone jewelry was pretty and trendy, and a small box on the site&#8217;s homepage mentioned that the brand used vermeil. But clicking further into the site, I realized its pages were devoid of descriptions—not even dinky bulleted lists.</p>\\n<p>Because of this, visitors to the site are left to wonder if the <em>silver</em> in the product titles means &#8220;sterling silver&#8221; or just &#8220;silver tone,&#8221; and if the opal-looking gem in the middle of a beautiful ring is an actual opal or a facsimile.</p>\\n<p>The well-designed site, which is clearly targeting Gen Zers, may be an extreme example of the Great Description Decline of 2021. But it speaks to a larger trend in e-commerce that&#8217;s seen brands downsize and demote descriptions in the name of…what? Making shopping speedier? Keeping pages &#8220;cleaner&#8221;? Does it makes sense to skeletonize (or altogether delete) product description for these, or any other, reasons?</p>\\n<p>Nope. And here&#8217;s why. People don&#8217;t buy products. Not really—they buy the promise of self-improvement. And when it comes to jewelry, they buy to align themselves with certain tribes, or gain entrée into nuanced clubs (i.e., the club of women wearing trendy paper clip chains, which right now includes every Instagram influencer under the sun).</p>\\n<p>And while gorgeous photography can usher jewelry lovers into that important &#8220;want it, need it, gotta have it&#8221; mindset, a creative (but brief and fact-filled) description has the power to romance them through traditional storytelling that layers meaning and context over a piece&#8217;s basic details.</p>\\n<p>There&#8217;s a reason social media jewelry influencers such as <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/gemgossip/?hl=en\" target=\"_blank\">Gem Gossip</a>’s Danielle Miele and <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/diamondsinthelibrary/?hl=en\" target=\"_blank\">Diamonds in the Library</a>’s Becky Stone sell so much jewelry, both their own and others&#8217;: They&#8217;re masters of spinning yarns around jewelry pieces to make them seem unique, special, and exciting.</p>\\n<p>A recent Diamonds in the Library <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/p/CJ6J0nohrPn/\" target=\"_blank\">post</a> showed an antique ring from Wilson&#8217;s Estate Jewelry featuring a carving of a woman&#8217;s face. Stone&#8217;s storytelling prowess was in full effect as she wrote: &#8220;This is The Empress. <span class=\"\">Resplendent with the ethereal glory of the Art Nouveau aesthetic, she is captivating, from her opal and ruby crown to the flowing gold locks of her hair and her carefully carved hardstone face.&#8221;</span></p>\\n<p>If you&#8217;re worried about having long chunks of text gunk up your pages, consider a collapsible section; consumers receptive to being romanced by terrific writing can access the text with a single click, while those in a hurry can skip it.</p>\\n<p>But I contend that few will. Jewelry is an investment, and while impulse buys happen in brick-and-mortar stores, my feeling is that women take their time when shopping online, and enjoy revisiting photos, texts, and details on a product page multiple times before finally hitting &#8220;add to cart.&#8221;</p>\\n<p>Give ’em something tantalizing to chew on.</p>\\n<p><em>(Photo: <a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/78656956@N06/9899159484\" target=\"_blank\">HM Revenue &amp; Customs</a>)</em></p>\\n<p><em><span class=\"s2\">Follow</span> <span class=\"s2\">Emili </span><span class=\"s2\">Vesilind</span> <span class=\"s2\">on Instagram:\\xa0</span><a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/emilivesilind/\" target=\"_blank\"><span class=\"s3\">@</span><span class=\"s3\">emilivesilind</span></a></em></p>\\n<strong>Follow JCK on Instagram:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/jckmagazine/\">@jckmagazine</a><br/>\\r\\n\\r\\n<strong>Follow JCK on Twitter:</strong> <a href=\"https://twitter.com/jckmagazine\">@jckmagazine</a><br/>\\r\\n\\r\\n<strong>Follow JCK on Facebook:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/JCKmagazine\">@jckmagazine</a>\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t \\n<div class=\"category_container data-pagebuilder=\"section-container\">\\n                        \\n                        \\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"row \" id=\"section-1-tab-1-row-1\" data-pagebuilder=\"row\">\\n                            \\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"col-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12    \" id=\"section-1-tab-1-row-1-column-1\" data-widget-type=\"default\" data-pagebuilder=\"column\">\\n                                \\n                                \\n                                \\n                                \\n                                    <!-- Widget (master) -->\\n\\n<div class=\"widget mb-30\" data-pagebuilder=\"widget\" data-widget-index=\"1\">\\n\\t<a href=\"javascript:void(0)\"  data-widget-url=\"\"  class=\"d-none widget-inner w-100 px-0  position-0 w-100 h-auto h-sm-100       {WIDGET_ICON_LINK_CLASS}\"  style=\"background-color: transparent;\" >\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t</a>\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t<span class=\\'content-block d-block w-100   \\' style=\\'background-color: transparent; \\' >\\n\\t\\t\\t<span class=\\'d-flex flex-column align-self-center w-100\\'><h1 class=\\'w-100 d-block text-left h1 h2 mb-3 \\' data-widget-element=\\'widgetHeader\\' data-pagebuilder=\\'element\\'>Marketing Tactics</h1><p class=\\'w-100 d-block text-left p lead mb-30 \\' data-widget-element=\\'widgetParagraph\\' data-pagebuilder=\\'element\\'>Spend your Digital Marketing Credits on a variety of tactics to help optimize performance and enhance your user-experience. Your digital marketing account manager will guide you in selecting which service to utilize according to the strategy derrived during onboarding. <a href=\\'https://meetings.hubspot.com/katie200\\'>Schedule a consultation</a> if you have any questions or would like to speak to someone about your options.</p>\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t</span>\\n\\t\\t\\t</span>\\n</div>\\n\\n                                \\n                                \\n                                \\n                            </div>\\n                        </div>\\n                        \\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"row \" id=\"section-1-tab-1-row-2\" data-pagebuilder=\"row\">\\n                            \\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t<div class=\"col-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12    \" id=\"section-1-tab-1-row-2-column-1\" data-widget-type=\"default\" data-pagebuilder=\"column\">\\n                                \\n                                \\n                                \\n                                \\n                                    <!-- Widget -->\\n\\n<div class=\"widget mb-30 d-block d-sm-flex mb-60\">\\n\\t<div class=\"section-title-icon\">\\t\\n\\t\\t<a href=\"javascript:void(0)\" class=\"d-block pmicon\"><i class=\"punch-edit-layout text-primary circle-border\"></i></a>\\n\\t</div>\\t\\n\\t<span class=\"section-title-content d-flex flex-column align-self-center h-100\">\\n\\t\\t<span class=\"section-title-content-wrap\"><h3 class=\\'w-100 d-block text-left h3 pt-1 \\' data-widget-element=\\'widgetHeader\\' data-pagebuilder=\\'element\\'>Content Creation</h3></span>\\n\\t\\t<span class=\"section-title-content-wrap\"><p class=\\'w-100 d-block text-left p lead mb-0 \\' data-widget-element=\\'widgetParagraph\\' data-pagebuilder=\\'element\\'>Ideally, every piece of content on your website will have an educational or entertainment value, while including specific keywords that drive the products and services of your business.
